Abstract: The growing deployment of small Unmanned Aerial Systems (sUASs) in low-altitude airspaces has increased the need for reliable tactical deconfliction under safety-critical constraints. Tactical deconfliction involves short-horizon decision-making in dense, partially observable, and heterogeneous multi-agent environments, where both cooperative separation assurance and operational efficiency must be maintained. While Large Language Models (LLMs) exhibit strong reasoning capabilities, their direct application to air traffic control remains limited by insufficient domain grounding and unpredictable output inconsistency. This paper investigates LLMs as decision-makers in cooperative multi-agent tactical deconfliction using fine-tuning strategies that align model outputs to human operator heuristics. We propose a simulation-to-language data generation pipeline based on the BlueSky air traffic simulator that produces rule-consistent deconfliction datasets reflecting established safety practices. A pretrained Qwen-Math-7B model is fine-tuned using two parameter-efficient strategies: supervised fine-tuning with Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and preference-based fine-tuning combining LoRA with Group-Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Experimental results on validation datasets and closed-loop simulations demonstrate that supervised LoRA fine-tuning substantially improves decision accuracy, consistency, and separation performance compared to the pretrained LLM, with significant reductions in near mid-air collisions. GRPO provides additional coordination benefits but exhibits reduced robustness when interacting with heterogeneous agent policies.

### [440] [StreamingVLA: Streaming Vision-Language-Action Model with Action Flow Matching and Adaptive Early Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28565)
*Yiran Shi,Dongqi Guo,Tianchen Zhao,Feng Gao,Liangzhi Shi,Chao Yu,ZhiJian Mo,Qihua Xiao,XiaoShuai Peng,Qingmin Liao,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了StreamingVLA模型，通过异步并行化视觉-语言-动作(VLA)各阶段，实现了速度和流畅性的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型虽然表现优异，但其高计算开销导致在边缘设备应用中效率低下，且各阶段必须串行，导致频繁停顿和高延迟，影响实际部署。

Method: 系统分析VLA模型效率瓶颈后，提出两项创新：(1) 用action flow matching取代chunk-based方法，实现动作生成与执行阶段的并行；(2) 设计动作显著性自适应观察机制，实现观测与执行阶段的并行。

Result: StreamingVLA能在不损失性能的前提下，实现2.4倍的时延加速、6.5倍的执行停顿减少。

Conclusion: StreamingVLA显著提升了VLA模型的执行速度与流畅性，有助于其在资源受限的实际场景下部署和应用。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models have demonstrated exceptional performance in natural language-driven perception and control. However, the high computational cost of VLA models poses significant efficiency challenges, particularly for resource-constrained edge platforms in real-world deployments. However, since different stages of VLA (observation, action generation and execution) must proceed sequentially, and wait for the completion of the preceding stage, the system suffers from frequent halting and high latency. To address this, We conduct a systematic analysis to identify the challenges for fast and fluent generation, and propose enabling VLAs with the ability to asynchronously parallelize across VLA stages in a "streaming" manner. First, we eliminate the reliance on action chunking and adopt action flow matching, which learns the trajectory of action flows rather than denoising chunk-wise actions. It overlaps the latency of action generation and execution. Second, we design an action saliency-aware adaptive observation mechanism, thereby overlapping the latency of execution and observation. Without sacrificing performance, StreamingVLA achieves substantial speedup and improves the fluency of execution. It achieves a 2.4 $\times$ latency speedup and reduces execution halting by 6.5 $\times$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: EBuddy系统将专家操作流程建模为有限状态机（FSM），以此为核心，将语音请求与当前流程状态及可执行动作绑定。系统通过ASR（自动语音识别）和意图理解，实现对多种异构资源（如GUI软件与协作机器人）的语音驱动协调。

Abstract: This paper presents EBuddy, a voice-guided workflow orchestrator for natural human-machine collaboration in industrial environments. EBuddy targets a recurrent bottleneck in tool-intensive workflows: expert know-how is effective but difficult to scale, and execution quality degrades when procedures are reconstructed ad hoc across operators and sessions. EBuddy operationalizes expert practice as a finite state machine (FSM) driven application that provides an interpretable decision frame at runtime (current state and admissible actions), so that spoken requests are interpreted within state-grounded constraints, while the system executes and monitors the corresponding tool interactions. Through modular workflow artifacts, EBuddy coordinates heterogeneous resources, including GUI-driven software and a collaborative robot, leveraging fully voice-based interaction through automatic speech recognition and intent understanding. An industrial pilot on impeller blade inspection and repair preparation for directed energy deposition (DED), realized by human-robot collaboration, shows substantial reductions in end-to-end process duration across onboarding, 3D scanning and processing, and repair program generation, while preserving repeatability and low operator burden.

### [442] [A Self-Rotating Tri-Rotor UAV for Field of View Expansion and Autonomous Flight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28581)
*Xiaobin Zhou,Zihao Zheng,Aoxu Jin,Lei Qiang,Bo Zhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了三旋翼自转无人机SPINNER，通过自旋运动扩展相机和激光雷达的视场，采用三电机和反扭板实现姿态与旋转独立控制。为应对旋转飞行带来的强耦合与复杂干扰，提出结合非线性模型预测控制与增量非线性动态反演的扰动补偿控制框架。

Abstract: Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) perception relies on onboard sensors like cameras and LiDAR, which are limited by the narrow field of view (FoV). We present Self-Perception INertial Navigation Enabled Rotorcraft (SPINNER), a self-rotating tri-rotor UAV for the FoV expansion and autonomous flight. Without adding extra sensors or energy consumption, SPINNER significantly expands the FoV of onboard camera and LiDAR sensors through continuous spin motion, thereby enhancing environmental perception efficiency. SPINNER achieves full 3-dimensional position and roll--pitch attitude control using only three brushless motors, while adjusting the rotation speed via anti-torque plates design. To address the strong coupling, severe nonlinearity, and complex disturbances induced by spinning flight, we develop a disturbance compensation control framework that combines nonlinear model predictive control (MPC) with incremental nonlinear dynamic inversion. Experimental results demonstrate that SPINNER maintains robust flight under wind disturbances up to 4.8 \,m/s and achieves high-precision trajectory tracking at a maximum speed of 2.0\,m/s. Moreover, tests in parking garages and forests show that the rotational perception mechanism substantially improves FoV coverage and enhances perception capability of SPINNER.

### [443] [Dynamic Lookahead Distance via Reinforcement Learning-Based Pure Pursuit for Autonomous Racing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28625)
*Mohamed Elgouhary,Amr S. El-Wakeel*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出将PPO强化学习与传统Pure Pursuit（PP）路径跟踪算法结合，实现动态调整lookahead距离，提高自动驾驶车辆在赛车场景下的性能。该方法兼具快速响应与曲线精度，超越了固定或简单自适应lookahead的传统做法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Pure Pursuit算法对lookahead参数极为敏感，固定值难以兼顾弯道精度和直道稳定性，限制了自动驾驶车辆的极限操控能力。为提升不同赛道、速度下的路径跟踪性能，亟需一种既能“懂”车辆状态又可动态调整参数的方法。

Method: 将PPO强化学习用于生成lookahead指令，输入为车辆速度和多视野曲率特征；训练过程在F1TENTH Gym仿真器进行，使用KL惩罚和学习率衰减提升稳定性。训练完成后，模型部署在ROS2环境，实时指导Pure Pursuit控制器。与固定和传统自适应lookahead的PP以及真实车辆进行对比实验。

Result: 仿真与实车实验均证明，学习到的lookahead控制策略能根据道路曲率和速度自适应调整——直道增大，弯道减小——有效提升圈速和稳定性，尤其在未见过的新赛道上表现最佳。此外，能承受更激进的速度配置，实验证明模型零次调试下可成功从仿真迁移至实车。

Conclusion: 融合强化学习与经典控制的自适应Pure Pursuit方案，在轨迹跟踪任务上兼具理解性、泛化性与性能提升。在线自适应单参数优化（lookahead）的方法，为自动驾驶实车控制和sim-to-real迁移提供了新思路和高效实现方式。

Abstract: Pure Pursuit (PP) is a widely used path-tracking algorithm in autonomous vehicles due to its simplicity and real-time performance. However, its effectiveness is sensitive to the choice of lookahead distance: shorter values improve cornering but can cause instability on straights, while longer values improve smoothness but reduce accuracy in curves. We propose a hybrid control framework that integrates Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with the classical Pure Pursuit controller to adjust the lookahead distance dynamically during racing. The PPO agent maps vehicle speed and multi-horizon curvature features to an online lookahead command. It is trained using Stable-Baselines3 in the F1TENTH Gym simulator with a KL penalty and learning-rate decay for stability, then deployed in a ROS2 environment to guide the controller. Experiments in simulation compare the proposed method against both fixed-lookahead Pure Pursuit and an adaptive Pure Pursuit baseline. Additional real-car experiments compare the learned controller against a fixed-lookahead Pure Pursuit controller. Results show that the learned policy improves lap-time performance and repeated lap completion on unseen tracks, while also transferring zero-shot to hardware. The learned controller adapts the lookahead by increasing it on straights and reducing it in curves, demonstrating effectiveness in augmenting a classical controller by online adaptation of a single interpretable parameter. On unseen tracks, the proposed method achieved 33.16 s on Montreal and 46.05 s on Yas Marina, while tolerating more aggressive speed-profile scaling than the baselines and achieving the best lap times among the tested settings. Initial real-car experiments further support sim-to-real transfer on a 1:10-scale autonomous racing platform

</details>


### [444] [Serialized Red-Green-Gray: Quicker Heuristic Validation of Edges in Dynamic Roadmap Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28674)
*Yulie Arad,Stav Ashur,Marta Markowicz,James D. Motes,Marco Morales,Nancy M. Amato*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效应对动态环境地图规划的方法，并展示了其在实际中的显著加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态环境中，如机器人仓库，障碍物位置频繁变化，传统基于路网的方法需频繁重建路网或大量碰撞检测，效率低下。如何快速适应环境变化，提高规划速度，是当前亟需解决的问题。

Method: 提出Red-Green-Gray (RGG) 框架，在SPITE的基础上，通过保守的几何近似将路网中的边分为无效（红）、有效（绿）和不确定（灰）三类。进一步设计了批量序列化与向量化的串行RGG（SerRGG）算法，实现高效GPU加速。

Result: 实验结果表明，RGG方法有效降低了需要完全验证的未知边数量，相较于传统串行实现，SerRGG在性能上提升2-9倍。

Conclusion: 结合了几何精度与计算速度，SerRGG方法在对时间要求严格的机器人应用中表现出色，适用于动态环境下的高效运动规划。

Abstract: Motion planning in dynamic environments, such as robotic warehouses, requires fast adaptation to frequent changes in obstacle poses. Traditional roadmap-based methods struggle in such settings, relying on inefficient reconstruction of a roadmap or expensive collision detection to update the existing roadmap. To address these challenges we introduce the Red-Green-Gray (RGG) framework, a method that builds on SPITE to quickly classify roadmap edges as invalid (red), valid (green), or uncertain (gray) using conservative geometric approximations. Serial RGG provides a high-performance variant leveraging batch serialization and vectorization to enable efficient GPU acceleration. Empirical results demonstrate that while RGG effectively reduces the number of unknown edges requiring full validation, SerRGG achieves a 2-9x speedup compared to the sequential implementation. This combination of geometric precision and computational speed makes SerRGG highly effective for time-critical robotic applications.

Conclusion: 该方法为稀土和关键原材料的本地循环和供应安全增强提供了技术路劲，也为精确和实时的物料流分析（MFA）实现提供了基础。

Abstract: Stable and reliable supplies of rare-Earth minerals and critical raw materials (CRMs) are essential for the development of the European Union. Hence, in this paper we present the preliminary phases of the development of real-time visual detection of PC desktop components running on edge devices to simultaneously achieve two goals. The first goal is to perform robotic disassembly of PC desktops, where the adaptivity of learning-based vision can enable the processing of items with unpredictable geometry caused by accidental damages. We also discuss the robot end-effectors for different PC components with the object contact points derivable from neural detector bounding boxes. The second goal is to provide in an autonomous, highly-granular, and timely fashion, the data needed to perform material flow analysis (MFA) since, to date, MFA often lacks of the data needed to accurately study material stocks and flows. The second goal is achievable thanks to the recently-proposed synchromaterials, which can generate both local and wide-area (e.g., national) material mass information in a real-time and synchronized fashion.

### [446] [DRIVE-Nav: Directional Reasoning, Inspection, and Verification for Efficient Open-Vocabulary Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28691)
*Maoguo Gao,Zejun Zhu,Zhiming Sun,Zhengwei Ma,Longze Yuan,Zhongjing Ma,Zhigang Gao,Jinhui Zhang,Suli Zou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的结构化探索框架DRIVE-Nav，用于解决开放词汇物体导航（OVON）中的高效路径规划与目标定位问题，显著减少重复探查和路径冗余，在多个主流数据集和实际机器人部署中取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本OVON方法在未知环境下，因仅能在稠密边界点上推理，导致路径选择不稳定、反复探查和冗余动作。如何提升探索效率、减少重复行动和提升导航成功率，是当前急需破解的问题。

Method: DRIVE-Nav用方向（而非原始边界）结构化探索过程，通过240度前视视角筛选决策方向，采用快速行进方法（FMM）提取方向候选，并维护代表性视图以进行视觉-语言语义检测和跨帧验证，从而提升目标地物体的识别、定位和路径规划效率。

Result: DRIVE-Nav在HM3D-OVON、HM3Dv2、MP3D等数据集上取得了显著性能提升，在HM3D-OVON上SR（成功率）为50.2%、SPL（路径长度标准化成功率）为32.6%，分别较前作提升1.9%和5.6%；在HM3Dv2和MP3D上获得了最佳SPL。在物理仿真和实物机器人上也验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: DRIVE-Nav通过结构化的方向探索策略，大幅提升了开放词汇物体导航中的路径效率和目标达成率，表现出强大的泛化性和现实部署潜力。

Abstract: Open-Vocabulary Object Navigation (OVON) requires an embodied agent to locate a language-specified target in unknown environments. Existing zero-shot methods often reason over dense frontier points under incomplete observations, causing unstable route selection, repeated revisits, and unnecessary action overhead. We present DRIVE-Nav, a structured framework that organizes exploration around persistent directions rather than raw frontiers. By inspecting encountered directions more completely and restricting subsequent decisions to still-relevant directions within a forward 240 degree view range, DRIVE-Nav reduces redundant revisits and improves path efficiency. The framework extracts and tracks directional candidates from weighted Fast Marching Method (FMM) paths, maintains representative views for semantic inspection, and combines vision-language-guided prompt enrichment with cross-frame verification to improve grounding reliability. Experiments on HM3D-OVON, HM3Dv2, and MP3D demonstrate strong overall performance and consistent efficiency gains. On HM3D-OVON, DRIVE-Nav achieves 50.2% SR and 32.6% SPL, improving the previous best method by 1.9% SR and 5.6% SPL. It also delivers the best SPL on HM3Dv2 and MP3D and transfers to a physical humanoid robot. Real-world deployment also demonstrates its effectiveness. Project page: https://coolmaoguo.github.io/drive-nav-page/

</details>


### [447] [SOLE-R1: Video-Language Reasoning as the Sole Reward for On-Robot Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28730)
*Philip Schroeder,Thomas Weng,Karl Schmeckpeper,Eric Rosen,Stephen Hart,Ondrej Biza*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了专为机器人强化学习奖励设计的视频-语言推理模型SOLE-R1，能够以视频和自然语言目标为输入，自动生成任务进展奖励，实现无需任何真实标签或人工指示下的机器人自主任务学习，并显著优于现有视觉语言评估器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型在部分可观测性和分布偏移情况下容易被策略利用其感知误差来“作弊”，无法可靠作为强化学习的奖励信号。作者旨在设计一个更鲁棒、对机器人任务更适用的奖励生成器。

Method: 提出SOLE-R1模型，基于原始视频和自然语言目标做逐时空链式推理，输出密集的任务进展估计。训练方法结合大规模合成视频轨迹和推理过程，采用监督微调和来自可验证奖励的强化学习混合训练框架。

Result: 在四个仿真环境和真实机器人场景中，SOLE-R1支持从随机初始化下的零样本在线强化学习，能完成24个未知操控任务，无需真实奖励、成功标签、示范或专用调参。

Conclusion: SOLE-R1作为强化学习奖励信号源显著优于当前最强视觉-语言奖励模型（包括GPT-5、Gemini-3-Pro），并对奖励“攻击”具有更高鲁棒性，为机器人自主学习任务带来新的技术路径。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown impressive capabilities across diverse tasks, motivating efforts to leverage these models to supervise robot learning. However, when used as evaluators in reinforcement learning (RL), today's strongest models often fail under partial observability and distribution shift, enabling policies to exploit perceptual errors rather than solve the task. To address this limitation, we introduce SOLE-R1 (Self-Observing LEarner), a video-language reasoning model explicitly designed to serve as the sole reward signal for online RL. Given only raw video observations and a natural-language goal, SOLE-R1 performs per-timestep spatiotemporal chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning and produces dense estimates of task progress that can be used directly as rewards. To train SOLE-R1, we develop a large-scale video trajectory and reasoning synthesis pipeline that generates temporally grounded CoT traces aligned with continuous progress supervision. This data is combined with foundational spatial and multi-frame temporal reasoning, and used to train the model with a hybrid framework that couples supervised fine-tuning with RL from verifiable rewards. Across four different simulation environments and a real-robot setting, SOLE-R1 enables zero-shot online RL from random initialization: robots learn previously unseen manipulation tasks without ground-truth rewards, success indicators, demonstrations, or task-specific tuning. SOLE-R1 succeeds on 24 unseen tasks and substantially outperforms strong vision-language rewarders, including GPT-5 and Gemini-3-Pro, while exhibiting markedly greater robustness to reward hacking.

</details>


### [448] [Pandora: Articulated 3D Scene Graphs from Egocentric Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28732)
*Alan Yu,Yun Chang,Christopher Xie,Luca Carlone*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文以人类佩戴智能眼镜自然探索场景时采集的第一视角数据，弥补机器人自身传感器无法探测的盲区，进而提升机器人的环境感知和操作能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器人地图构建主要依赖自身的传感器及相机，受限于自身结构和能力，难以完整探索和建模环境中的部分区域（如抽屉、墙柜等）。这些限制导致所建地图不完整，需要更高能力的机器人来补全。本文旨在突破此局限，提高环境图的完整性和语义丰富度。

Method: 通过让人类佩戴Project Aria智能眼镜，自然探索场景，获取第一视角的“egocentric”数据。借助简单启发式方法，分析和转换这些数据以重建环境中可运动的对象部件，并将其集成到三维场景图表示中，进而补足机器人自身难以探测的空间和动态信息。

Result: 本文方法利用人类视角采集的数据，恢复出高质量的可运动对象部件模型，效果与依赖其它输入形式的先进方法相当。此外，将这些模型融入三维场景图后，显著提升了机器人对对象动态以及容器-对象关系的理解。

Conclusion: 结合人类第一视角数据，可显著拓展和增强现有机器人对场景的理解与操作，提升机器人执行如检索隐藏物品等任务的能力，无需依赖高端硬件。本方法为将人类探索知识有效迁移至各种机器人提供了途径。

Abstract: Robotic mapping systems typically approach building metric-semantic scene representations from the robot's own sensors and cameras. However, these "first person" maps inherit the robot's own limitations due to its embodiment or skillset, which may leave many aspects of the environment unexplored. For example, the robot might not be able to open drawers or access wall cabinets. In this sense, the map representation is not as complete, and requires a more capable robot to fill in the gaps. We narrow these blind spots in current methods by leveraging egocentric data captured as a human naturally explores a scene wearing Project Aria glasses, giving a way to directly transfer knowledge about articulation from the human to any deployable robot. We demonstrate that, by using simple heuristics, we can leverage egocentric data to recover models of articulate object parts, with quality comparable to those of state-of-the-art methods based on other input modalities. We also show how to integrate these models into 3D scene graph representations, leading to a better understanding of object dynamics and object-container relationships. We finally demonstrate that these articulated 3D scene graphs enhance a robot's ability to perform mobile manipulation tasks, showcasing an application where a Boston Dynamics Spot is tasked with retrieving concealed target items, given only the 3D scene graph as input.

</details>


### [449] [FocusVLA: Focused Visual Utilization for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28740)
*Yichi Zhang,Weihao Yuan,Yizhuo Zhang,Xidong Zhang,Jia Wan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了FocusVLA，一种能有效聚焦于任务相关视觉信息以提升动作生成质量的新视觉-语言-动作模型；通过创新注意力机制，有效缓解现有VLA模型在细节利用和注意力分配方面的关键瓶颈，并在多项机器人实验中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型受限于架构偏差、视觉token过多和无关视觉噪声，导致模型无法充分利用关键视觉细节，严重影响动作生成质量。作者旨在系统性分析这些瓶颈，并寻找更有效的视觉信息利用方式以推动VLA模型性能提升。

Method: 作者首先实证分析了当前模型利用视觉信息的主要问题。随后，提出FocusVLA，主包含两大创新：一是模态级联注意力（Modality Cascaded Attention）消除捷径通路，强制模型依赖任务相关视觉细节；二是焦点注意力机制（Focus Attention），动态筛选和权衡任务相关视觉patch，抑制无关干扰噪声，控制输入信息量。

Result: FocusVLA在仿真和现实机器人基准任务上均展现出更好地利用视觉细节、提升动作生成准确率和收敛速度的能力，相较现有方法有显著性能提升。

Conclusion: 该工作证明，合理利用并聚焦任务相关视觉信息，是突破VLA动作生成性能瓶颈的关键手段。FocusVLA通过新型注意力机制大幅提升了多任务机器人操作能力，并为后续视觉-语言-动作模型设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models improve action generation by conditioning policies on rich vision-language information. However, current auto-regressive policies are constrained by three bottlenecks: (1) architectural bias drives models to overlook visual details, (2) an excessive number of visual tokens makes attention difficult to focus on the correct regions, and (3) task-irrelevant visual information introduces substantial noise - together severely impairing the quality of action. In this paper, we investigate how to effectively utilize different visual representations for action generation. To this end, we first empirically validate the above issues and show that VLA performance is primarily limited by how visual information is utilized, rather than by the quality of visual representations. Based on these insights, we introduce FocusVLA, a novel paradigm that directs the model's attention to task-relevant visual regions to effectively bridge vision to action. Specifically, we first propose Modality Cascaded Attention to eliminate shortcut pathways, thereby compelling VLA models to rely on task-relevant visual details for action generation. Furthermore, we propose Focus Attention, which dynamically selects task-relevant visual patches to control information quantity while explicitly modulating their influence to suppress task-irrelevant noise. Extensive experiments on both simulated and real-world robotic benchmarks demonstrate that FocusVLA not only effectively leverages visual details to perform dexterous manipulations, but also substantially improves performance and accelerates convergence across a variety of tasks.

</details>
